 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:3px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>AMAZON.COM ANNOUNCES FIRST QUARTER SALES UP 34% TO $13.18 BILLION; </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>16 OF THE TOP 100 BESTSELLING TITLES ARE EXCLUSIVE TO THE KINDLE STORE </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">SEATTLE&#151;(BUSINESS WIRE)&#151;April 26, 2012&#151;Amazon.com, Inc. (NASDAQ: AMZN) today announced financial results for its first quarter ended March&nbsp;31, 2012. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Operating cash flow increased 1% to $3.05 billion for the trailing twelve months, compared with $3.03 billion for the trailing twelve months ended
March&nbsp;31, 2011. Free cash flow&nbsp;decreased 39% to $1.15 billion for the trailing twelve months, compared with $1.90 billion for the trailing twelve months ended March&nbsp;31, 2011. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Common shares outstanding plus shares underlying stock-based awards totaled 464&nbsp;million on March&nbsp;31, 2012, compared with 466&nbsp;million a year ago. During the quarter, the Company repurchased
5.3&nbsp;million shares, or $960 million, under its previously announced authorization to repurchase up to $2 billion of the Company&#146;s common stock. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Net sales increased 34% to $13.18 billion in the first quarter, compared with $9.86 billion in first quarter 2011. Excluding the $56 million unfavorable impact from year-over-year changes in foreign
exchange rates throughout the quarter, net sales would have grown 34% compared with first quarter 2011. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Operating income was $192 million in
the first quarter, compared with $322 million in first quarter 2011. The unfavorable impact from year-over-year changes in foreign exchange rates throughout the quarter on operating income was $4 million. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Net income decreased 35% to $130 million in the first quarter, or $0.28 per diluted share, compared with net income of $201 million, or $0.44 per diluted
share, in first quarter 2011. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;I&#146;m excited to announce that we now have more than 130,000 new, in-copyright books that are
exclusive to the Kindle Store &#151; you won&#146;t find them anywhere else. They include many of our top bestsellers &#151; in fact, 16 of our top 100 bestselling titles are exclusive to our store,&#148; said Jeff Bezos, founder and CEO of
Amazon.com. &#147;If you&#146;re an Amazon Prime member, you don&#146;t even need to buy these titles &#151; you can borrow them for free &#151; with no due dates &#151; from our revolutionary Kindle Owners&#146; Lending Library. The Kindle
Owners&#146; Lending Library is heavily used by Kindle owners, and it has extremely unusual features that both authors and customers love. Every time you borrow a book, the author gets paid &#151; and we have an inexhaustible supply of each title so
you never have to wait in a queue for the book you want. Kindle is the bestselling e-reader in the world by far, and I assure you we&#146;ll keep working hard so that the Kindle Store remains yet another reason to buy a Kindle!&#148; </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Highlights </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Kindle Fire remains the #1 bestselling, most gifted, and most wished for product across the millions of items available on Amazon.com since
launch.&nbsp;In the first quarter, 9 out of 10 of the top sellers on Amazon.com were digital products &#150; Kindle, Kindle books, movies, music and apps. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>About Amazon.com </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Amazon.com, Inc.
(NASDAQ: AMZN), a Fortune 500 company based in Seattle, opened on the World Wide Web in July 1995 and today offers Earth&#146;s Biggest Selection. Amazon.com, Inc. seeks to be Earth&#146;s most customer-centric company, where customers can find and
discover anything they might want to buy online, and endeavors to offer its customers the lowest possible prices. Amazon.com and other sellers offer millions of unique new, refurbished and used items in categories such as Books; Movies,
Music&nbsp;&amp; Games; Digital Downloads; Electronics&nbsp;&amp; Computers; Home&nbsp;&amp; Garden; Toys, Kids&nbsp;&amp; Baby; Grocery; Apparel, Shoes&nbsp;&amp; Jewelry; Health&nbsp;&amp; Beauty; Sports&nbsp;&amp; Outdoors; and Tools,
Auto&nbsp;&amp; Industrial. Amazon Web Services provides Amazon&#146;s developer customers with access to in-the-cloud infrastructure services based on Amazon&#146;s own back-end technology platform, which developers can use to enable virtually any
type of business. The new latest generation Kindle is the lightest, most compact Kindle ever and features the same 6-inch, most advanced electronic ink display that reads like real paper even in bright sunlight. Kindle Touch is a new addition to the
Kindle family with an easy-to-use touch screen that makes it easier than ever to turn pages, search, shop, and take notes &#150; still with all the benefits of the most advanced electronic ink display. Kindle Touch 3G is the top of the line e-reader
and offers the same new design and features of Kindle Touch, with the unparalleled added convenience of free 3G. Kindle Fire is the Kindle for movies, TV episodes, music, books, magazines, apps, games and web browsing with all the content, free
storage in the Amazon Cloud, Whispersync, Amazon Silk (Amazon&#146;s new revolutionary cloud-accelerated web browser), vibrant color touch screen, and powerful dual-core processor. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Amazon and its affiliates operate websites, including www.amazon.com, www.amazon.co.uk, www.amazon.de, www.amazon.co.jp, www.amazon.fr, www.amazon.ca, www.amazon.cn, www.amazon.it, and www.amazon.es. As
used herein, &#147;Amazon.com,&#148; &#147;we,&#148; &#147;our&#148; and similar terms include Amazon.com, Inc., and its subsidiaries, unless the context indicates otherwise. </FONT></P>

<DESCRIPTION>INFORMATION REGARDING NON-GAAP FINANCIAL MEASURES
<TEXT>
<HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>Information Regarding Non-GAAP Financial Measures</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Exhibit 99.2 </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Non-GAAP Financial Measures </I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Regulation G, <I>Conditions for Use of
Non-GAAP Financial Measures</I>, and other SEC regulations define and prescribe the conditions for use of certain non-GAAP financial information. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Our measure of &#147;Free cash flow&#148; meets the definition of a non-GAAP financial measure. Free cash flow is used in addition to and in conjunction with results presented in accordance with GAAP and
free cash flow should not be relied upon to the exclusion of GAAP financial measures. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Free cash flow, which we reconcile to
&#147;Net cash provided by (used in) operating activities,&#148; is cash flow from operations reduced by &#147;Purchases of fixed assets, including internal-use software and website development.&#148; We use free cash flow, and ratios based on it,
to conduct and evaluate our business because, although it is similar to cash flow from operations, we believe it typically will present a more conservative measure of cash flows since purchases of fixed assets are a necessary component of ongoing
operations. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Free cash flow has limitations due to the fact that it does not represent the residual cash flow available for
discretionary expenditures. For example, free cash flow does not incorporate payments made on capital lease obligations or cash payments for business acquisitions. Therefore, we believe it is important to view free cash flow as a complement to our
entire consolidated statements of cash flows. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">For a quantitative reconciliation of free cash flow to the most directly
comparable amounts reported in accordance with GAAP, see &#147;Supplemental Financial Information and Business Metrics&#148; in Exhibit 99.1 to this Current Report on Form&nbsp;8-K. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;Return on Invested Capital&#148; is a ratio based on free cash flow, and as such, is also a non-GAAP financial measure.&nbsp;Return
on invested capital is trailing twelve months free cash flow divided by average &#147;Total assets&#148; minus &#147;Current liabilities&#148; (excluding the current portion, if any, of our Long Term Debt), over the most recent five quarter
ends.&nbsp;We believe return on invested capital is a useful measure in assessing whether we are utilizing our capital efficiently.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">As with free cash flow, return on invested capital is used in addition to and in conjunction with results presented in accordance with GAAP and return on invested capital should not be relied upon to the
exclusion of GAAP financial measures.&nbsp;We include return on invested capital, and the denominator used to calculate it (called &#147;Invested Capital&#148;) in &#147;Supplemental Financial Information and Business Metrics&#148; in Exhibit 99.1
to this Current Report on Form&nbsp;8-K.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The effect on our consolidated statements of operations from changes in exchange
rates versus the U.S.&nbsp;Dollar is also a non-GAAP financial measure. Information regarding the effect of exchange rates, versus the U.S.&nbsp;Dollar, on our consolidated statements of operations is provided to show reported period operating
results had the exchange rates remained the same as those in effect in the comparable prior year period. We include various measures on both an as-reported basis and a basis showing the effect of changes in exchange rates versus the U.S. dollar in
&#147;Supplemental Financial Information and Business Metrics&#148; in Exhibit 99.1 to this Current Report on Form 8-K. </FONT></P>
